                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Thursday, July 7, 2011
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UWWfrgo5bgY/ThXwj4AUQKI/AAAAAAAAKzU/l7BX0-6Updk/s320/1.JPG" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="8951037002205218538" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="3052747859868965012" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="3052747859868965012">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     Betty White NUDE!
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3052747859868965012" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UWWfrgo5bgY/ThXwj4AUQKI/AAAAAAAAKzU/l7BX0-6Updk/s1600/1.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UWWfrgo5bgY/ThXwj4AUQKI/AAAAAAAAKzU/l7BX0-6Updk/s320/1.JPG" width="255"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <b>
                      Betty White Ludden
                     </b>
                     (born January 17, 1922), better known as
                     <b>
                      Betty White
                     </b>
                     , is an American actress,
                     <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comedienne" title="Comedienne">
                      comedienne
                     </a>
                     ,  author, and former game show personality. With a career spanning nine  decades since 1939, she is best known to modern audiences for her  television roles as
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sue_Ann_Nivens" title="Sue Ann Nivens">
                      Sue Ann Nivens
                     </a>
                     on
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Mary_Tyler_Moore_Show" title="The Mary Tyler Moore Show">
                       The Mary Tyler Moore Show
                      </a>
                     </i>
                     and
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rose_Nylund" title="Rose Nylund">
                      Rose Nylund
                     </a>
                     on
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Golden_Girls" title="The Golden Girls">
                       The Golden Girls
                      </a>
                     </i>
                     . As of 2010, she is starring as
                     <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elka_Ostrovsky" title="Elka Ostrovsky">
                      Elka Ostrovsky
                     </a>
                     in the
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TV_Land" title="TV Land">
                      TV Land
                     </a>
                     sitcom
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hot_in_Cleveland" title="Hot in Cleveland">
                       Hot in Cleveland
                      </a>
                     </i>
                     .  She has also released several books over the span of her career. In  August 2010, she entered a deal with G.P. Putnam Sons to produce two  more books, the first of which was scheduled for release in 2011.
                     <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Betty_White#cite_note-1">
                       <span>
                       </span>
                       <span>
                       </span>
                      </a>
                     </sup>
                     <br/>
                     White has won seven
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emmy_Award" title="Emmy Award">
                      Emmy Awards
                     </a>
                     and received 20 Emmy nominations
                     <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thr_2-0">
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Betty_White#cite_note-thr-2">
                       <span>
                       </span>
                      </a>
                     </sup>
                     over the course of her career, including being the first woman ever to receive an Emmy for
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daytime_Emmy_Award_for_Outstanding_Game_Show_Host" title="Daytime Emmy Award for Outstanding Game Show Host">
                      game show hosting
                     </a>
                     (for the short-lived
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Just_Men%21" title="Just Men!">
                       Just Men!
                      </a>
                     </i>

                     </a>
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live" title="Saturday Night Live">
                       Saturday Night Live
                      </a>
                     </i>
                     , for which she also received a
                     <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award" title="Primetime Emmy Award">
                      Primetime Emmy Award
                     </a>
                     . She made regular appearances on the game shows

                      <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Password_%28TV_series%29" title="Password (TV series)">
                       Password
                      </a>

                       Match Game
                      </a>
                     </i>

                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mama%27s_Family" title="Mama's Family">
                       Mama's Family
                      </a>
                     </i>
                     ,
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boston_Legal" title="Boston Legal">
                       Boston Legal
                      </a>
                     </i>
                     , and
                     <i>
                      <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Bold_and_the_Beautiful" title="The Bold and the Beautiful">

                      </a>
                     </i>
